     546                 :            :          * work around a problem where PE lookups might be
     547                 :            :          * done before Linux has established valid PE's

     549                 :            :          * Linux has been fixed to always setup valid PEs.
     550                 :            :          *

     557                 :            :          * FF, things will go bad. We need to ensure we don't

    3493                 :          8 : static bool phb3_wait_dlp_reset(struct phb3 *p)

    3498                 :            :         /*
    3499                 :            :          * Firmware cannot access the UTL core regs or PCI config space
    3500                 :            :          * until the cores are out of DL_PGRESET.
    3501                 :            :          * DL_PGRESET should be polled until it is inactive with a value
    3502                 :            :          * of '0'. The recommended polling frequency is once every 1ms.
    3503                 :            :          * Firmware should poll at least 200 attempts before giving up.
    3504                 :            :          * MMIO Stores to the link are silently dropped by the UTL core if
    3505                 :            :          * the link is down.
    3506                 :            :          * MMIO Loads to the link will be dropped by the UTL core and will
    3507                 :            :          * eventually time-out and will return an all ones response if the
    3508                 :            :          * link is down.
    3509                 :            :          */
    3510                 :            : #define DLP_RESET_ATTEMPTS      40000
    3511                 :            :

    3516                 :            :                         break;
    3517                 :          0 :                 time_wait_us(10);
    3518                 :            :         }

    3522                 :            :         }
    3523                 :            :         return true;
